[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing run detected a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m issue when [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing an M3U8 playlist. The fuzzer-triggered code attempted an outbound TCP [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection to jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m, which was flagged by the SSRF sanitizer. This [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates that untrusted or external URLs in playlist content can provoke network [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequests, potentially exposing internal services or sensitive data.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue: During fuzz testing, the parser invoked java.net.Socket and [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjava.net.HttpURLConnection to retrieve remote resources. The SSRF sanitizer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m intercepted an attempted connection to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjazzer.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m and raised `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side Request Forgery [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type: Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Untrusted input [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontrolling destination endpoints may lead to unauthorized network access or data [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexfiltration.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace shows the connection attempt originates in [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.tika.parser.m3.M3U8Parser.handleLink`, which uses [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mHttpURLConnection.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to fetch linked resources.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer rules in [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.ServerSideRequestForgery` flag any [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutbound socket or HTTP connections.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer entry point is `com.example.M3U8ParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich calls `parseOne` on arbitrary input, leading to potential external fetches.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The reported deduplication token [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`b782adc79e9c6729`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m suggests this input [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern has been seen before and categorized as an SSRF risk.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.tika.parser.m3.M3U8Parser` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially `handleLink` and `_parse` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to understand how URLs are processed and fetched.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The use of `TikaInputStream.get` and subsequent `HttpURLConnection` [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls—review how the parser opens remote connections.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness in `com.example.M3U8ParserFuzzer` to see how test inputs are [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupplied and whether network fetches can be disabled or sandboxed.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Configuration or hardening points in the networking layer [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., URL protocols[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowed, connection timeouts, host whitelisting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to get a holistic view of how [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal resources are handled.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m600[0m[39m:        String path = [0m[1;35murl.getPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m601[0m[39m:        int slash = [0m[1;35mpath.lastIndexOf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'/'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m602[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mslash + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m < [0m[1;35mpath.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m works even with [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m![0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m603[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaCoreProperties.RESOURCE_NAME_KEY, [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mpath.substring[0m[1;39m([0m[39mslash + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m604[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m605[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m606[0m[39m:        String type = [0m[1;35mconnection.getContentType[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m607[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtype != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m608[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMetadata.CONTENT_TYPE, type[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m609[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m610[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m611[0m[39m:        String encoding = [0m[1;35mconnection.getContentEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m612[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mencoding != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m613[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMetadata.CONTENT_ENCODING, encoding[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m614[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m615[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m616[0m[39m:        int length = [0m[1;35mconnection.getContentLength[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m617[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m618[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMetadata.CONTENT_LENGTH, [0m[1;35mInteger.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m619[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m620[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m621[0m[39m:        return new [0m[1;35mTikaInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mBufferedInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mconnection.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m622[0m[39m:                new [0m[1;35mTemporaryResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, length, [0m[1;35mgetExtension[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmetadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m623[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The SSRF vulnerability stems from `[0m[1;35mM3U8Parser.handleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` unconditionally [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreating a `new [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhen the line starts with “http”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and calling [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mURL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This always opens a network connection via [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`URLConnection`, enabling untrusted input to direct outbound HTTP/S requests.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must preserve the ability to record playlist links in metadata [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mmetadata.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK, nextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and still allow embedded‐content parsing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen explicitly desired, but by default prevent automatic network fetches to close [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe SSRF hole.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-Level Fix[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce a parser-specific configuration object or flag in the `ParseContext`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g. `M3U8ParserConfig.allowExternalLinks`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that controls whether external [0m[1;35mHTTP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mS[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetches are performed.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By default, this flag is false [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnetwork fetch disabled[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malways add the link to metadata, but will early‐return before making any network [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall unless `allowExternalLinks` is explicitly set to true.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Document the new configuration and provide guidance to downstream users on how[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto enable remote fetching if genuinely needed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith understanding of SSRF [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplications[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Define a Configuration Holder[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Add a new class, e.g.:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m tika-parsers-standard-modules/[0m[33m...[0m[35m/[0m[95mM3U8ParserConfig.java[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        package org.apache.tika.parser.m3;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        import org.apache.tika.parser.ParseContext;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        public class M3U8ParserConfig [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[39m** By default false: no automatic [0m[1;35mHTTP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fetch of playlist links. *[0m[35m/[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            private final boolean allowExternalLinks;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            public [0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mthis[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            public [0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean allowExternalLinks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                this.allowExternalLinks = allowExternalLinks;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            public boolean [0m[1;35misExternalLinksAllowed[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return allowExternalLinks;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[39m** Retrieve from context, defaulting to disallow. *[0m[35m/[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            public static M3U8ParserConfig [0m[1;35mfrom[0m[1;39m([0m[39mParseContext context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                M3U8ParserConfig cfg = [0m[1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mM3U8ParserConfig.class[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return cfg != null ? cfg : new [0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Guard the Network Call in [0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In `[0m[1;35mM3U8Parser.handleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, after the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextLine.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m164[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m retrieve parser config from context:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        M3U8ParserConfig cfg = [0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig.from[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcfg.isExternalLinksAllowed[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m do not open network connections; leave the link in metadata only[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This block must precede the creation of `new [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and use of [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. The rest of the existing embedded‐content logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m174[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged and only executes when external fetch is explicitly [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menabled.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Documentation & Examples[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Update the Javadoc for `M3U8Parser` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mclass‐level[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `[0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmention:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • The default behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno [0m[1;35mHTTP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fetch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • How to enable by calling `[0m[1;35mcontext.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mM3U8ParserConfig.class, new [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mM3U8ParserConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` prior to parsing.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Add a note in the TikaParser manual/CHANGELOG about this new opt-in flag to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent SSRF by default.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Testing & Compatibility[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Existing unit tests that simply parse an M3U8 string without remote [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresources will be unaffected [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe metadata is still populated[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Tests that do expect remote embedded parsing must be updated to set [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in the context. Alternatively, add a new integration test [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargeting remote fetch behavior under the new config.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - No changes are made to the Jazzer harness or any consumer tests; the fuzzer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill no longer trigger a network call, and the SSRF sanitizer will not fire.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification & Side-Effect Analysis[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By gating the network fetch behind an explicit flag, we close the SSRF [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability for all unmodified consumers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand the fuzzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while preserving the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mability for advanced users to fetch external playlist segments when they [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsciously opt in.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach leaves all existing metadata‐recording and embedded‐content [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing logic intact. We do not remove functionality, only require an explicit [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mopt-in.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change is fully backwards‐compatible in the sense that code which never [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mset the flag sees no new exceptions—`[0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` simply returns earlier.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential side effect: consumers who relied on automated fetching must now [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicitly enable it. We mitigate this by documenting the change prominently in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelease notes.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. References and Similar Patterns[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This pattern mirrors how other Tika parsers handle optional network or [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal‐resource fetching [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., the `ImageParser` allowing external entity [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution via a context flag[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external libraries or fuzz harness modifications are needed—everything is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontained within the `tika-parsers` module. [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In the link-handling loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m162[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it inserts:  [0m                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify Root Cause:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All compilation errors stem from the fact that the new class [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`M3U8ParserConfig` does not exist in the codebase.  The import and the code that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences this class in `M3U8Parser.java` therefore cannot resolve the symbol.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Create `M3U8ParserConfig` in the Same Module:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Under the directory  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `tika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maudiovideo-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/m3/`  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     add a new file `M3U8ParserConfig.java` with package declaration [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.tika.parser.m3`.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Implement a standard parser-configuration pattern consistent with other Tika [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser modules:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. A private boolean field `externalLinksAllowed` defaulting to `false`.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Public getter `[0m[1;35misExternalLinksAllowed[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and setter [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msetExternalLinksAllowed[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c. A static factory method `[0m[1;35mfrom[0m[1;39m([0m[39mParseContext ctx[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` that:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Attempts to retrieve an existing instance from [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mctx.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mM3U8ParserConfig.class[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - If `null`, constructs a new `M3U8ParserConfig`, registers it in the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontext [0m[1;39m([0m[39moptional[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and returns it.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures that `[0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig.from[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` always returns a non-null [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfig object and that users of the parser can override the default via [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparseContext.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mM3U8ParserConfig.class, customConfig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Reapply the SSRF-guard Patch in `M3U8Parser.java`:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - At the top of the file, add:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `import org.apache.tika.parser.m3.M3U8ParserConfig;`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the `[0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, after verifying [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnextLine.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, insert:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         M3U8ParserConfig cfg = [0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig.from[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcfg.isExternalLinksAllowed[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Abort external fetch when not permitted[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This preserves the original logic for non-HTTP or internal links while [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblocking untrusted external [0m[1;35mHTTP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fetches by default.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No Changes to Fuzz Harness or Tests:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Because the issue is confined to the missing configuration class in the parser[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodule, no modifications to the Jazzer harness, other external libraries, or test [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode are necessary.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests and fuzz targets will continue to run; they will now receive a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault `[0m[33mexternalLinksAllowed[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m` and will not attempt outbound connections, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthus eliminating the SSRF finding.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Validate and Build:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run `mvn clean compile` on the `tika-parser-audiovideo-module` to confirm [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. The new class is discovered.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. The import and references in `M3U8Parser.java` resolve correctly.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run the full Tika build [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mvn install -[0m[33mDskipTests[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregressions in other modules.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By adding `M3U8ParserConfig` in the same package and module, we directly resolve [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe symbol-not-found compilation errors.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The configuration pattern follows existing Tika parser conventions, ensuring [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistency and future extensibility.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Defaulting `externalLinksAllowed` to false closes the SSRF vector without [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisabling legitimate embedded-content parsing of local or relative links.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tests, harnesses, and overall parser logic remain unchanged except for the new [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard, so existing functionality is fully preserved and no broad-catch or harness [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtweaks are introduced.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mM3U8ParserConfig.class[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and returns a default instance when null.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Implement java.io.Serializable, define serialVersionUID.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. This ensures that [0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig.from[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m compiles and returns a valid[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfig.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Update M3U8Parser.java to wire in the new configuration class.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Add the import at the top of the file:  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.apache.tika.parser.m3.M3U8ParserConfig;  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In [0m[1;35mhandleLink[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, before opening network streams, retrieve and honor the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfig flag. Replace the existing network-fetch block with:  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mmetadata.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK, nextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mnextLine.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Guard against SSRF: only fetch external links if explicitly allowed[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      M3U8ParserConfig cfg = [0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig.from[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcfg.isExternalLinksAllowed[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      EmbeddedDocumentExtractor ex = [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mEmbeddedDocumentUtil.getEmbeddedDocumentExtractor[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m … proceed with [0m[1;35mTikaInputStream.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextLine[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m …[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. No other logic in handleLink is modified—only the insertion of the config [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Verify build and runtime behavior.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • By default, [0m[33mexternalLinksAllowed[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m: all “http” URIs in playlists will be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecorded as metadata [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but not fetched—preserving security and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreventing SSRF.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Consumers who wish to allow external fetches can do so by configuring the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser:  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     M3U8Parser parser = new [0m[1;35mM3U8Parser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     M3U8ParserConfig cfg = new [0m[1;35mM3U8ParserConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mcfg.setExternalLinksAllowed[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mparser.setM3U8ParserConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcfg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcontext.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mM3U8ParserConfig.class, cfg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • No changes are needed to harness or test code; tests depending on embedded [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetch remain unchanged because the default behavior mirrors no-fetch.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserve existing functionality:  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • All non-HTTP URI handling remains untouched.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Metadata collection [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPLAY_LIST_LINK entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continues unaltered.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Only HTTP fetches are now subject to an explicit allow-list flag.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side effects and mitigation:  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Default users will not fetch any remote segments, which is safer. If any unit [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests implicitly expect remote fetches, they must be updated to set [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [33mexternalLinksAllowed[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m via ParseContext. However, no existing tests in Tika [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectly fetch real HTTP URIs in M3U8 parsing, so breakage is unlikely.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Document the new configuration option in the module’s README or javadoc.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References and consistency:  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Follows the pattern of PDFParserConfig [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parser-pdf-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/pdf/PDFParserConfig.jav[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Leverages [0m[1;35mParseContext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mT.class[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m semantics for parser-specific settings.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Does not modify fuzzer harness, test harness, or external [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies—complies with project guidelines.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
